     function launchWindow(url, features,x,y) {
     	var xMax = screen.width, yMax = screen.height;
     	// var xOffset = (xMax - x)/2, yOffset = (yMax - y)/2;
     	var xOffset = 1, yOffset = 1;
         if (features=='') {
     	    var Neufenster =window.open(url, "_blank", 'height='+y+',width='+x+',innerHeight='+y+',innerWidth='+x+',screenX=0,screenY=0,top='+yOffset+',left='+xOffset+',toolbar=0,menubar=0,allwaysRaised,location=0, scrollbars=yes,reziable=no,fullscreen=no,channelmode=no');
     	} else {
     	    var Neufenster =window.open(url, "_blank", 'height='+y+',width='+x+',innerHeight='+y+',innerWidth='+x+',screenX=0,screenY=0,top='+yOffset+',left='+xOffset+',toolbar=0,menubar=0,allwaysRaised,location=0, scrollbars=yes,fullscreen=no,channelmode=no,'+features);
     	}
     	// Neufenster.scrollbars.visible=false;
     }
     
     
     function launchWindow_maxsize(url,features) {
 		url =check_url_for_flash_blaettermix(url);
         launchWindow(url, features,screen.width, screen.height)
     }
     
 	function check_url_for_flash_blaettermix(url) {
 		if (!hasFlash) {
 			// url = url.replace("index.html", "pubData/mobile/index.htm"); 
 		}
 		return(url);
 	}
 
     function get_client_height() {
       var myWidth = 0, myHeight = 0;
       if( typeof( window.innerWidth ) == 'number' ) {
         //Non-IE
         myWidth = window.innerWidth;
         myHeight = window.innerHeight;
       } else if( document.documentElement && ( document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.documentElement.clientHeight ) ) {
         //IE 6+ in 'standards compliant mode'
         myWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
         myHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
       } else if( document.body && ( document.body.clientWidth || document.body.clientHeight ) ) {
         //IE 4 compatible
         myWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
         myHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
       }
       return myHeight;
     }
 
     function mix_setcookie(cookiename, cookievalue) {
         var ablauf = new Date();
         var inTagen = ablauf.getTime() + (1 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
         ablauf.setTime(inTagen);
        
         document.cookie = cookiename+"="+cookievalue+"; expires=" + ablauf.toGMTString();
     }
     
     
     function mix_readcookie( cookiename ) {
         var mycookiewerte = document.cookie.split(";");
         var mycookie = "";
         for (var i=0;i<mycookiewerte.length;i++) {
             mycookie = mycookiewerte[i].split("=");
             mycookie[0] = mycookie[0].replace(/ /g, "");
             // alert(mycookie[0]+":"+mycookie[1]);
             if ( mycookie[0] == cookiename ) {
                         return ( mycookie[1] ); 
             }
         }
     }
 
     //
     // Orangen Balken auf Fensterlänge ziehen
     //
     function set_orange_content2_height() {
         var h1 = document.getElementById('content1').offsetHeight;
         var h2 = document.getElementById('content2').offsetHeight;
 
         // Innere Fenster Größe bestimmen
         var h = get_client_height(); 
 
         // wenn innerer Content kleiner als rechter balken, dann rechten balken auf Fenstergröße setzen
         if (h1<h) {h1=h+10;}
         
         // wenn rechter balken kleiner als zuvor bestimmt, dann größer machen
         if (h1>document.getElementById('content2').offsetHeight) {
             var c2 = document.getElementById('content2');
             c2.style.height=h1+"px";
         }
 
         // wenn Menu Balken kleiner als zuvor bestimmt, dann größer machen
         if (h1>document.getElementById('menu').offsetHeight) {
             var c2_menu = document.getElementById('menu');
             h1 = Math.max( h1, document.getElementById('content2').offsetHeight );
             c2_menu.style.height=h1+"px";
         }
     }
     
     function set_orange_menu_height() {
         var h1 = document.getElementById('content1').offsetHeight;
         var h2 = document.getElementById('content2').offsetHeight;
         // Innere Fenster Größe bestimmen
         var h = get_client_height(); 
         // wenn innerer Content kleiner als rechter balken, dann rechten balken auf Fenstergröße setzen
         if (h1<h) {h1=h+10;}
         // wenn rechter balken kleiner als zuvor bestimmt, dann größer machen
         if (h1>document.getElementById('menu').offsetHeight) {
             var c2 = document.getElementById('menu');
             c2.style.height=h1+"px";
         }
     }
     
     
     function set_orange_content2_horoskop_height() {
         var h1 = document.getElementById('content1').offsetHeight;
 
         // Innere Fenster Größe bestimmen
         var h = get_client_height(); 
 
         // wenn innerer Content kleiner als rechter balken, dann rechten balken auf Fenstergröße setzen
         if (h1<h) {h1=h+10;}
 
         if (h1>document.getElementById('content2_horoskop').offsetHeight) {
             var c2 = document.getElementById('content2_horoskop');
             c2.style.height=h1+"px";
             // c2.style.height="150%";
         }
 
         // wenn Menu Balken kleiner als zuvor bestimmt, dann größer machen
         if (h1>document.getElementById('menu').offsetHeight) {
             var c2_menu = document.getElementById('menu');
             h1 = Math.max( h1, document.getElementById('content2_horoskop').offsetHeight );
             c2_menu.style.height=h1+"px";
         }
     }
     
     //
     // Get Window-Scrolled Position
     // http://www.softcomplex.com/docs/get_window_size_and_scrollbar_position.html
     // 
     function f_scrollLeft() {
     	return f_filterResults (
     		window.pageXOffset ? window.pageXOffset : 0,
     		document.documentElement ? document.documentElement.scrollLeft : 0,
     		document.body ? document.body.scrollLeft : 0
     	);
     }
     function f_scrollTop() {
     	return f_filterResults (
     		window.pageYOffset ? window.pageYOffset : 0,
     		document.documentElement ? document.documentElement.scrollTop : 0,
     		document.body ? document.body.scrollTop : 0
     	);
     }
     function f_filterResults(n_win, n_docel, n_body) {
     	var n_result = n_win ? n_win : 0;
     	if (n_docel && (!n_result || (n_result > n_docel)))
     		n_result = n_docel;
     	return n_body && (!n_result || (n_result > n_body)) ? n_body : n_result;
     }

   <script>
    function acceptCookies() {
 	Cookies.set('datenschutz', 'ok', {expires: 365*2});
 	$(".cookie-advice").hide();
 }
 function openCookies() {
 	window.open("/rechtliches.php", "cookies", "width=500,height=700");
 }
 if (Cookies.get('datenschutz') != "ok") $(".cookie-advice").show();
   </script>

     <!--
 
     toggle_rubriken = 'allon';
 
     /**
     * check_rubriken(o)
     * .. check/uncheck all checkboxes with "rubrik" in it's name
     */
     function check_rubriken(what) {
         
         var e_anz = document.mixtour.length;
         for (var i = 0; i < e_anz; ++i) {
           if (document.mixtour.elements[i].name.substr(0,6) == "rubrik" ) {
                 if (what=="allon") {
                     document.forms[0].elements[i].checked=true;
                 } else {
                     document.forms[0].elements[i].checked=false;
                 }
           }
         }
         
         // Toggle switch
         if ( what == "allon" ) {
             toggle_rubriken = "alloff";
         } else {
             toggle_rubriken = "allon";
         }
         
         return false;
         
     }
     
     
     
     /**
     * set_uhrzeit(o)
     * .. schiebt den Bis Select auf zwei Felder weiter
     * .. merkt sich die werte im Cookie
     */
     function set_uhrzeit(o) {
         var o2 = document.getElementById("search_uhrzeit_bis");
     
         //
         // auswahl eins = beliebig
         //
         if ( o.selectedIndex == 0 ) { 
             o2.selectedIndex = 0; 
         }
         else {
             //
             // alles andere als beliebig
             //
             if (o.selectedIndex+1>o2.length-1){
                 // o2.selectedIndex = o.selectedIndex+2-o2.length; 
             } else {
                 o2.selectedIndex = o.selectedIndex+1 
             }
         }
         setcookie();
     }
     
     // 
     // Cookie Functions
     //
 
     function setcookie() {
         var ablauf = new Date();
         var infuenfTagen = ablauf.getTime() + (1 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
         ablauf.setTime(infuenfTagen);
         
         // alert("stichwort:"+document.getElementById("stichwort").value );
         document.cookie = "stichwort="+document.getElementById("stichwort").value+"; expires=" + ablauf.toGMTString();
         document.cookie = "uhrab="+document.getElementById("search_uhrzeit_ab").selectedIndex+"; expires=" + ablauf.toGMTString();
         document.cookie = "uhrbis="+document.getElementById("search_uhrzeit_bis").selectedIndex+"; expires=" + ablauf.toGMTString();
         // umland1 umland2 umland4
         // document.getElementById("umland1").
         // alert( document.getElementById("stichwort").value );
     }
     
     
     function readcookie() {
         var mycookiewerte = document.cookie.split(";");
         var mycookie = "";
         for (var i=0;i<mycookiewerte.length;i++) {
             mycookie = mycookiewerte[i].split("=");
             mycookie[0] = mycookie[0].replace(/ /g, "");
             // alert(mycookie[0]+":"+mycookie[1]);
             switch(mycookie[0]) {
                 case "stichwort":  
                     if ( document.getElementById("stichwort").value.length==0 && !(!mycookie[1]) ) { 
                         document.getElementById("stichwort").value = mycookie[1]; 
     //                    if (!mycookie[1]) {
     //                        document.getElementById("stichwort").value = ''; 
     //                    }
                     }; 
                     break;
                 case "uhrab":
                     document.getElementById("search_uhrzeit_ab").selectedIndex = mycookie[1];
                     break;
                 case "uhrbis":
                     document.getElementById("search_uhrzeit_bis").selectedIndex = mycookie[1];
                     break;
                     
                     
             }
         }
     }
     
     function urlMenuMonat(that) {
         setcookie();
     	// var theURL = "mixtour_kalender.php?monat="+that.options[that.selectedIndex].value;
     	var theURL = "index_mixtour.php?monat="+that.options[that.selectedIndex].value;
     
     	if (theURL) {
     		window.location = theURL;
     	}
     }

         <script language="JavaScript1.2" type="text/javascript">
          <!-- Hide Script from old browser
 var x = 0;
 function MehrInfo(name)
 {
 if ( x > 0) { if (karte.closed == false) { karte.close(); } x = 0; }
 karte = window.open("mixtour_karteikarte.php3?verort="+name+"","","width=320,height=370,scrollbars=YES,resizable=yes,screenX=70,screenY=70");
 karte.focus();
 x = 1;
 }
 
 var loaded = 0;
 var gotlayers = 0;
 var lastbutton='top';
 
 
 var NS4 = (document.layers) ? 1 : 0;
 var IE4 = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
 var ver4 = (NS4 || IE4) ? 1 : 0;
 
 
 function popUp(menuName,on) {
 		if (gotlayers) {
 				if (on) {
 						if (NS4) {
 								document.layers[menuName].visibility = "show";
 						} else {
 								document.all[menuName].style.visibility = "visible";
 						}
 				} else {
 						if (NS4) {
 								document.layers[menuName].visibility = "hide";
 						} else {
 								document.all[menuName].style.visibility = "hidden";
 						}
 				}
 		}
 }
 
 //-->
         </script>

 karte.focus();
 x = 1;
 }

   f = window.open(url, "trailer", "width=1020,height=600,left=50,top=50,scrollbars=yes, location=no");
   f.focus();
 }
